echo psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"Error: "#"错误："#g' psftp.c
# "did not receive SFTP response packet from server"
# "unable to understand SFTP response packet from server: %s"
# "psftp: not connected to a host; use \"open host.name\"\n"
# "psftp: already connected\n"
# "open: expects a host name\n"
# "open: invalid port number\n"
# "lcd: expects a local directory name\n"
# "lcd: unable to change directory: %s\n"
# "New local directory is %s\n"
# "Current local directory is %s\n"
# "help: %s: command not found\n"
# "Fatal: unable to initialise SFTP: %s\n"
# "Warning: failed to resolve home directory: %s\n"
# "Remote working directory is %s\n"
# "Fatal: unable to open %s\n"
# "all PSFTP agent requests should be synchronous"
# "Received unexpected end-of-file from SFTP server"
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"PuTTY Secure File Transfer (SFTP) client\n"#"PuTTY 安全文件传输 (SFTP) 客户端\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"Usage: psftp [options] [user@]host\n"#"用法: psftp [选项] [用户名@]主机\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"Options:\n"#"选项:\\n"#g' psftp.c

perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -bc       output batchfile commands\n"#"  -bc       输出批处理文件命令\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -be       don'\''t stop batchfile processing if errors\n"#"  -be       批处理文件发生错误也不停止其处理进程\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -v        show verbose messages\n"#"  -v        显示详细信息\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -load sessname  Load settings from saved session\n"#"  -load 会话名  载入保存的会话信息\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -l user   connect with specified username\n"#"  -l 用户名 使用指定的用户名连接\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -P port   connect to specified port\n"#"  -P 端口   连接指定的端口\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -pw passw login with specified password\n"#"  -pw 密码  使用指定的密码登录\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -1 -2     force use of particular SSH protocol version\n"#"  -1 -2     强制使用 SSH 协议版本\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -4 -6     force use of IPv4 or IPv6\n"#"  -4 -6     强制使用 IPv4 或 IPv6 版本\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -C        enable compression\n"#"  -C        允许压缩\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -i key    private key file for user authentication\n"#"  -i 密钥   认证使用的密钥文件\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -noagent  disable use of Pageant\n"#"  -noagent  禁止使用 Pageant 认证代理\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -agent    enable use of Pageant\n"#"  -agent    开启使用 Pageant 认证代理\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"            manually specify a host key (may be repeated)\n"#"            手工指定主机密钥指纹 (可能是重复的)\\n"#g' psftp.c
perl -i -pe 's#\Q"  -batch    disable all interactive prompts\n"#"  -batch    禁止所有交互提示\\n"#g' psftp.c
